   namaḥ śaśikalākārabrahmasūtrāṃśuśobhine /	namaH SaSi-kalA-AkAra-brahmasUtra-aMSu-SoBine /
   śritāya haṃsakāntyeva saṃparkārkamalaukasaḥ // Bhmj_19.*18 //	SritAya haMsakAnti-eva saMparka-arkam-ala-okasaH // Bhmd-_19.*18 //
   namo vidyānadīpūrṇaśāstrābdhisakalendave /	namaH vidyA-nadI-pUrNa-SAstra-abDi-sakala-indave /
   pīyūṣarasasārāya kavivyāpāravedhase // Bhmj_19.*19 //	pIyUza-rasa-sArAya kavi-vyApAra-veDase // Bhmd-_19.*19 //
   namaḥsatyanivāsāya svavikāśavilāsine /	namaH-satya-nivAsAya sva-vikASa-vilAsine /
   vyāsāya dhāmne tapasāṃ saṃsārāyāsahāriṇe // Bhmj_19.*20 //	vyAsAya DAmne tapasAm saMsAra-AyAsa-hAriNe // Bhmd-_19.*20 //
   ***** vyāsāṣṭakastotram || 51 || *****	***** vyAsa-azwaka-stotram || 51 || *****
   iti vyāsāṣṭakaṃ kṛtvā mahābhāratamañjarīm /	iti vyAsa-azwakam kRtvA mahABArata-maQjarIm /
   sacakre vibudhānandasudhāsyandataraṅgiṇīm // Bhmj_19.*21 //	sa-cakre vibuDa-Ananda-suDA-syanda-taraFgiNIm // Bhmd-_19.*21 //
   samāpteyaṃ mahābhāratamañjarī kṛtiḥ kavervyāsadāsāpanāmnaḥ	samAptA-iyam mahABArata-maQjarI kRtiH kaveH-vyAsat-AsApanAmnaH
   prakāśendrasūnoḥ kṣemendrasya ||	prakASa-indra-sUnoH kzemendrasya ||
   aho kavisarasvatyā vicitreyaṃ prasannatā /	aho kavi-sarasvatyA vicitrA-iyam prasanna-tA /
   sadyo malinatā vaktre khalānāṃ jāyate yayā // Bhmj_19.**1 //	sadyas malina-tA vaktre KalAnAm jAyate yayA // Bhmd-_19.**1 //
   madvacodarpaṇatale mahābhāratadigdvipaḥ /	mad-vacA-udarpaNa-tale mahABArata-diS-dvipaH /
   samastāvayavo 'pyeṣa muṣṭimeya ivekṣyate // Bhmj_19.**2 //	samasta-avayavaH api-eza muzwi-meyaH iva-Ikzyate // Bhmd-_19.**2 //
   ratnodāracatuḥsamudraraśanāṃ bhuktvā bhuvaṃ kauravo bhagnoruḥ patitaḥ sa	ratna-udAra-catur-samudra-raSanAm BuktvA Buvam kOravaH Bagna-UruH patitaH sa
   niṣparijane jīvanvṛkairbhakṣitaḥ /	nizparijane jIvan-vRkEH-BakzitaH /
   gaupairviśvajayī jitaḥ sa vijayaḥ kakṣaiḥ kṣitā vṛṣṇayastasmātsarvamidaṃ	gOpEH-viSva-jayI jitaH sa vijayaH kakzEH kzitAH vRzNayaH-tasmAt-sarvam-idam
   vicārya suciraṃ śāntyai mano dīyatām // Bhmj_19.**3 //	vicArya su-ciram SAntyE manaH dIyatAm // Bhmd-_19.**3 //
   phullendīvarasundaradyutimuṣaḥ śaureḥ śarīratviṣaḥ	Pulla-indIvara-sundara-dyuti-muzaH SOreH SarIra-tvizaH
   pāyāsurnijanābhipaṅkajarajolubdhālimālopamāḥ /	pAya-asuH-nija-nABi-paFkaja-rajaH-lubDa-ali-mAla-upamAH /
   yāḥ kurvanti śaśāṅkabimbaviṣade lakṣmīmukhābje muhuḥ	yAH kurvanti SaSAFka-bimba-vizade lakzmI-muKa-abje muhur-
   kastūrīrasapattrabhaṅgasubhagā lakṣmīmukhābje muhaḥ	kastUrI-rasa-pattra-BaFga-suBagA lakzmI-muKa-abje muhar-
   kastūrīrasapattrabhaṅgasubhagā lakṣmīprabhāvibhramam // Bhmj_19.**4 //	kastUrI-rasa-pattra-BaFga-suBagA lakzmI-praBA-viBramam // Bhmd-_19.**4 //
   eṣa viṣṇukathātīrthapuṇyavatsalilokṣitaḥ /	eza vizNu-kaTA-tIrTa-puNya-vat-salila-ukzitaH /
   prāptaḥ sāmānyajalpo 'pi kṣemendro 'dya kavīndratām // Bhmj_19.**5 //	prAptaH sAmAnya-jalpaH api kzemendraH adya kavi-indra-tAm // Bhmd-_19.**5 //
   || śubhaṃ bhūyat ||	|| SuBam BUyat ||
